резред рдореБрдйреНрдйреБрд░реИ

рекреи-рд╡рджреБ

F-реи

рд╡рд┐рд▓реНрд▓рд┐рд╡рд▓рдореН рд╢реНрд░реА рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдорд┐рдпрд┐рдйреН

F-рен

реирем

Biography of Villivalam Narayanacharya Swami

(Vangipuram Navaneetam Sri Ramadesikacharya,

Oppiliyappa Sannidhi)

рез. Preface

I, a learned devotee, undertake this endeavor, bearing the appointment of the Supreme Lord to draw a brief biography of that great man, Sri Upa Villivalam Narayanacharya Swami, who was the embodiment of the Supreme Being, the embodiment of wisdom, detachment, and detachment, and who was the protector of the divine vision by understanding the Vishishtadvaita philosophy. I, the devotee of the Supreme Lord, undertake this endeavor, bearing the appointment of the Supreme Lord on my head, to draw a brief biography of that great man, for inclusion in the edition of the wonderful work Paramatapanga Vyakyana. No matter how the article is structured, there is no fault in being satisfied that I have fulfilled the appointment of the Mahabhagavata!

реи. Who are the Paramaikandi?

Other.

The word Paramaikandi has been used in our Darshan since time immemorial. The word refers to one who practices good ethics and performs Vedic rituals according to the rules of the scriptures. The true meaning is

Those who consider Lord Srimannarayana as the supreme deity and do not even think of any other deity in their hearts are Ekandi. Those who do not seek any benefit from Him except salvation are Paramaikandi. Those who do not seek any other benefit in this time and do not consider salvation as a result of it and are immersed in the experience of the qualities of the Lord are Paramaikandi. This distinction was explained to us by Sri Desikan.

реи

Villivalam Sri Swami’s

рей. What is the place where good people should live?

The scriptures tell us the appropriate place for such Paramaikandi to live here while performing Kainkaryam. The holy lands such as Aryavartha, which the Dharmakas had mentioned as places for them to live, have fallen into the hands of the Viparitas in this Kaliyuga and are no longer suitable for the Sattvics to live. Now, when we look for a suitable place to live and perform Kainkaryam, the places where the Bhagavatas reside are the best and the scriptures have already given us the final verdict. ‘Live happily here in this sacred place until your body passes away’ is the divine decree given to the great sage, who had taken refuge in the Lord. This statement also indicates other places where the Lord has appeared, as the Acharyas have decided. Leaving aside all thoughts of a holy place - a divine country, it is better to live in such places and do whatever is possible for the Lord and His followers, leaving aside the idea of a divine land, and to do good deeds for the Lord and His followers. All these are the truths that our Desikan has seen and spoken about.

рек. The specialty of Thondai Nadu

Thondai Nadu has the unique honor of having incarnated the original ancestors of our darshan, the Mudalalwars, the Pradhan Acharyas, the Lord and Sri Desikan. The great men who have studied the Vedas and Vedantas can be found in Thondai Mandal more than in any other country. Desikan himself proudly calls them ‘Thondai Mandal Vedia’. That may also be the result of the Swami’s patriotism. We have no room for ambition! May the Cholanad be satisfied with the incarnation of the Nath Munis - Alavanthar - and other Azhwars who guided our vision!

рел. Speciality of the village of Pazhaveri

Pazhaveri Sri village is the best place for the rituals and practices of the Vedikas and for solitary residence. Many great people, who had studied the Vedas according to the Shastra system, had mastered the Vedanta knowledge and were immersed in the experience of the Lord, lived in this village with great respect and many astikas tried to make this village their home. Among the great people who lived permanently in this village, there was a noble family that had been practicing as Srotris for generations.

Summary of history

рей

Sri Upa. This historical leader, Narayanacharya Swami, was born as the first son of Arundhava to Narasimhacharya Swami and his wife, Param Sadhvi Ranganayaki.

рем. Appearance of Swami in Villivalam

The nearby Sri village of Villivalam is also famous for its great people. This Sri village, which was proud of the glory of Pazhaveri village, made itself the place for the incarnation of this historical leader and attracted that glory. Is this all? He made him forget his ancestral village and made himself an epithet for the Swami and gave him the title ‘Villivalam Swami’ and had to be satisfied with the feeling that Pazhaveri village was his original place anyway.

It was gone.

рен. The Youth of the Charitait Leader

The appearance of Villivalam Swami on the full moon day of the month of Aadi in the year Nala. The glorious Thirunakshatra, in which the first Acharya to incarnate in this world, Nammalvar, and Acharya Senai Mudaliar, were incarnated, became the birth star of Swami! Is this also a sign of the Sampradaya Pravartanam that Swami is going to perform? Even from a worldly perspective, there is something special about this day. Swami’s appearance was on August резрелth in the English year резрепрезрем. Is this a symbol of the independence that will come to India later and the speciality of celebrating this Swami’s English appearance day as a national festival every year? Nallan Chakravara in the Srivatsa clan

The special name of the temple is known as рддрд░реНрджрд┐, and the special appearance of this Swami is not surprising. It is needless to mention that he, who was born in a very high Vedic lineage, underwent Vedic rituals up to Upanayanam without fail in accordance with the Shastra system. This young man received the Thiruvazhi Thiruchangal from the hands of Srimad Alagyasinghar, who adorned the forty-ninth Asthanam, and also received mantra upadesha.

рео. Educational training

Since our young man’s father was a great scholar, he started studying with his father. He trained excellent teachers with a high Sampradaya system and with the clear

wisdom of Villivalam Sri Swami, he studied the basic knowledge of that time with his father. At that time, it was customary for the children of the Vedic clan who did not have the opportunity to study the Vedas in full to recite at least important parts of the Vedas. Similarly, the necessary amount of Vedas study was also done for our youth.

реп. Tarka Shastra training

The main goal for our youth was Vedanta Kalakshepa. To become fully qualified for it, his heart went into the training of Nyaya Shastra, which was the main effort. Thirumalaiyappan enrolled our youth as students in the Tirupati Sri Venkateswara Sanskrit College, which has great scholars, Upadhyayas. Tarka Shastra training is carried out with full enthusiasm. The teachers who became his teachers were great scholars, Purisai Anandan Pillai Sri Upa. Krishnamacharya Swami, Abhinava Desika Uttamur Sri Upa. Veeraragavacharya Swami. Thiruvarangam Sri Upa. Tirumalai Dadacharya Swami etc. Who else do you need? It is a great honor for the Acharyas to get intelligent disciples with great diligence. The teachers were amazed at the intellectual capacity and interest in learning of this disciple. It is the worldly way for disciples to focus on acquiring knowledge for themselves. This disciple, while grasping things, learned with the intention of becoming a training body to teach not only himself but also others, so the special nature of the training is not given. Since the youth was in the Shiromani class, he got the opportunity to study only the Nyaya scriptures prescribed by the university for that group.

резреж. Shastrapyasam even in his spare time

The youth had a desire to learn the upper parts of Nyaya Shastra that were not included in the examination. The Lord also allowed that. There are two or three vacations in the college every year! It is the nature of students to come to their hometown and spend their vacations with enthusiasm during those vacations. This student, however, has the desire to study the teacher during those vacations to learn the upper parts of the Nyaya Shastra. Nearby is the Sri village of Navalpakkam. As soon as he hears the name of the town, he gives glory to that town and becomes a great scholar with a great wealth of devotion and inexhaustible resources. The memory of Aiya Devanatha Dadacharya Swami comes to his mind and is sweet. The young man approached that Swami and worshipped him and made his

application. Sri Upa, who has the honor of making many disciples scholars by taking the knowledge of Jnana as his main object, The special wisdom imparted by Aiya Swami during his retreats, along with his supreme grace, enabled him to emerge as the first in the university examinations held in резрепрейрео.

резрез. Acharyascrayanam-Kalakshepam

"

Our youth has acquired the full competence to excel in the Nyaya Shastra and the Samusita Jnanaam in the Mimamsa. What is there to do now? To acquire the knowledge of Vedanta. Other Shastras are the means for that and to develop knowledge! It is the conclusion of the Brahmanas that studying Shastras that explain things other than the Lord is only to show one’s ability and does not guide the soul to the path of life! Should we search for a new Acharya? In the Srimad Ahobila Math, adorned with the рекрезst Divyastha, and endowed with the qualities of the celestial sign, Sausilyam, Saulabyam, etc., he took refuge at the feet of Srimad Alagyasingar, and by that grace, he attained the Srimad Our youth acquired perfect knowledge in Rahasyatrayasaram - Sri Geetabhashyam - Bhagavatvishyam. At the hands of that Srimad Alagyasingar, he performed Paranyasa at the feet of Alagyasingar and became a Krutakrutya, the Krutarthar, his Villivalam Swami. From now on, it is only by giving him the name Swami that we accept our form.

резреи. Sribhashya Kalakshepam

рекреиnd

The Sribhashya Kalakshepam remained for Villivalam Swami. It was Srilaxmindusimhan Sankalpam that Injimedu Srimad Alagyasingar, who had risen to the throne, was made Sribhashya Acharya to this Swami. Adopting the Shastra system, Villivalam Swami took up residence in the Gurukul and drank the Sribhashya nectar flowing from the mouth of Srimad Alagyasingar Thiruvakki and became deeply immersed in his soul. This Swami’s devotion increased due to the ability of the Avachariyan, who examined the subject matter in all the necessary places and gave him the principles and principles. Just as with the Lord, the Acharya’s devotion to the devotee

will be imprinted in his heart, and even more so with the Lord, the Acharya’s devotion to the devotee

will be manifested in his heart, even if it is implied that the Acharya’s teachings will be manifested in his heart.

As the story suggests, our Villivalam Swami’s boundless devotion to the Acharya

Special Acharya also highlighted many rare and authentic Brahmanical things that were not included in his teachings. Srimad Alagya Singha, seeing the devotion, the greatness of his disciple, the perfection of his intellect and the perfection of his soul, was filled with boundless joy and bestowed upon him all the essences of philosophy that lay within him, making him a perfect authority. Thus Villivalam Swami appeared and within реирей years, he became highly proficient in the general sciences and Vedanta, and from his youth he engaged in the sadhasara and the karma-nushkana that had been passed down through the family system, and with the excellence of his knowledge, he shone as a sattvic brahmacharya with such pride that anyone who saw him would respect him.

резрей. Entering the household

Many good people sought to take this groom of such a Vedic nature as their doctor. That was the time when Vedic nature was respected.

Marriage is a matter of finality; shouldn’t many aspects be considered in deciding a marriage? Lakshmi Nrusimhan took the initiative to have the daughter of a saintly man, who had been worshipping his feet without any fault, married to Villivalam Swami. He was the father of Bangipuram Devanathacharya Swami. That Swami wanted to give his daughter, Senbhagavalli, as his bride. The beautiful singer of Injimedu and the beautiful singer were very happy that they had a perfect relationship in all aspects. In those days, the method of ‘seeing and loving, speaking and marrying’ was not seen! The wedding took place on a very auspicious day, thanks to the presence of his father-in-law.

резрек. Grihastha Dharma Paripalanam

The scriptures praise the household very highly. The scriptures praise the household as the one who creates other ashrams and the household that has the right to entertain and feed guests is superior to other ashrams that make one stay as a guest. Our Villivalam Swami understood this truth well and started to maintain a household according to its greatness without following the shastras. In the Gita, where Kann─Бpraс╣Зa describes all things as the body of the Lord, he also says that he is a lust that does not contradict dharma. As if Sri Bhashyakara, who was in the ascetic life, had tried to explain this idea, our countryman, who led the household, explained in the

Summary of History

рен

‘Love for one’s wife is a lust that is not contrary to Dharma’. Considering all these truths, Villivalam Swami, having taken his wife as a gift from Sri Nrusimha, with great love and affection, greatly appreciated and accepted her assistance in his daily and regular duties such as karmanushtanam and Bhagavataratanam, and without fail, along with his Devi, he took care of the household without fail in the five-year duties of abhasanam and vaishvadevam.

резрел. Having children

The principle of accepting a family in order to perform the appropriate dharmas and to obtain good people has been adopted by the scriptures. Since the word ‘putra’ means one who protects the parents from entering the hell called ‘bud’, the principle of having a son is necessary to some extent adopted by the scriptures, but since this obligation applies only to those who are not the Supreme Being, the Sakalacharyas have also concluded, based on the Prapathi Shastra, that there is no obligation to have children in the case of the Supreme Being. The act of grace, however, states that having people who live by bowing to the feet of the Lord is a beneficial outcome. Thinking that giving this Swami a large family would hinder his intention to perform the worldly service through her, Sri Nrusimha blessed him with only a good daughter. In keeping with the Swami’s qualifications, he also married Maruga, a well-educated man of the highest Vedic lineage, and was pleased to give them good children. This act of greatness may also be the result of selfishness.

резрем. Residence and pilgrimage to the Mannar temple

He has acquired as much knowledge as he needs in the Shastras, especially in Vedanta. His household is also conducted according to the Shastras. He has also had a child according to the worldly system. Then, the priest who had invited Paramapathanathan to his temple, Villivalam Swami, performed the Kaingaryam for him in the form of Ajna Kaingaryam with devotion. In this situation, without being caught by the divine words of the Azhwars in the Mannar temple, Gopalan, who, with his beauty and charm, attracted all living beings, including scholars and laymen, and was fully experienced by many Asthanapatis, many Acharyas, Yatheeshwars and other great people, had a desire. The desire was to invite Villivalam Swami, who is considered a perfect authority by all means, to his presence and to show off his beauty so that both of them could experience it together. He was also a man who longed to have the best authorities who could experience him! He devised a strategy. At the very entrance of his Sannidhi, Lakshminrusimhan Thiruvu Srimad Alagyasingar entered the temple to get the opportunity to be worshipped by Villivalam Swami at the hands of Sri Ahobila Math, where he lived. The appointment was made immediately. Immediately, Villivalam Swami joined the Mannar Kovil and began the Sri Nrusimhan Thiruvaradhana, and lived contentedly, occasionally experiencing Gopalan. Did he find rest there too? Seeing the Swami’s great wisdom and abundance of goodness, many students approached the Swami and prayed to him to offer them Jnanapradhana. The Swami also happily agreed and performed Kavyam-Dadagam-Alangaram-Sastram according to their ability and desire. Over time, seeing the growth of Swami’s fame, many elderly devotees who had retired from high positions, determined to attain old age only with the wealth of knowledge, sought out and prayed to Swami, who was much younger than them, and spent time on matters of the Lord, etc., and felt greatly blessed. Villivalam Swami also became completely satisfied with the wealth he had received as a gift and ran a family. In this way, our Villivalam Swami lived in peace in the shadow of Gopalan, the object of the Brahmanas, and Sri Nrusimha, the Brahmanas that show him, in various ways, for two and a half years.

резрен. Sri Madhurantakam College Teacher

Injimedu Srimad Alagyasingar was on a pilgrimage and it happened that Gopalan Thiruvadi Varaha happened to visit. At that time, Srimad Alagyasingar saw the excellence of Villivalam Swami’s life, the way he imparted knowledge to many students, and how he shone as the object of great respect for many devotees. His grace towards Villivalam Swami increased. At the Sri Malola Vidvat Sadassa, which was the first time he had taken the form of a deity in Srirangam, he had blessed him with a special grace by appreciating the style of his speech. The Lord was pleased to place such a high authority in a place that was more conducive to the best performance of his duties. In this situation, Ramabran also had an aspiration.

Summary of the story

реп

That was to keep this Swami, who was immersed in the experience of Gopala, under his wing and impart his own experience. Then, as Srimad Alagya Singha was appointed, he was to accept the post of Vice-Chancellor in the Sanskrit Maha Kalasala, which was founded by him in Sri Madhurantakam and which is very famous, and to produce many scholars using his special knowledge and pravasana skill. Our Villivalam Swami worshipped Gopala, who had immersed himself in the ocean of sorrow for two and a half years and given him his complete experience, thanked him and received the appointment and joined Sri Madhurantakam. Even though the Swami agreed to this out of pride for his homeland, there was nothing wrong in that! After greeting Ramapriyan, who had invited him with love, with auspicious words, Srimad Alagya Singhar accepted the position of Vice-Principal in the Sanskrit College as per the divine order.

резрео. Pravasana Sathuryam

When Villivalam Swami arrived there and accepted the position, the enthusiasm of the students could not be contained. The important study of Tarkshastra, which is the main practice for learning Vedanta, began with enthusiasm. It is not an exaggeration to say that many young officers who are now scholars and succeed in speaking in assemblies are the fortunate ones who received the Shastra Grahana from Villivalam Swami. The speciality of listening patiently to whatever doubts the students may have, whether they are valid or not, and dispelling them with advice and guidance is rare to find elsewhere. It is difficult to estimate how many scholars the Swami created during the long period he sat in that place. It is a unique feature of the Swami that he starts to practice the upper parts only after seeing in each student whether the parts of the scriptures he explains have been absorbed in the hearts of the students. We see that many scholars who studied with the Swami are still enjoying the skill of practice that is not found in others and the wealth of knowledge they have acquired through it. The fact that he was honored with the silver jubilee for the great service he rendered to the community of scholars who had been sitting in that same college for twenty-five years and was blessed by the divine grace of Rama Pran Kadaksha and Srimad Alagya Singhar.

резреп, Still Getting an Acharya to Grahanam Vedanta

It is a common saying that no matter how much education a scholar has, he will never be satisfied. The Sruthi also says that one should develop knowledge further by listening to many Acharyas and in various ways. After many scholars accepted him as a skilled scholar who had acquired a firm mastery in logic and Vedanta, Villivalam Swami felt a burning desire to delve into those Shastras again and see their depths. Sri Nrusimha conceived the most suitable opportunity for this. At that time, a great man who had risen to the position of the head teacher in the very college where he was a teacher, That opportunity came when I got to read some scriptures on Vedanta. Who was that great man? That great man, who dared to speak the holy name of that Swami, and the entire Sri Vaishnava community was given the title ‘Thirukottiyur Swami’ along with the divine land where the Swami incarnated. Trying to convey the glory of that Swami to me is like trying to show the sun with a flashlight. However, in the midst of the great scholar’s centenary celebration, I, a little scholar, wrote an article about the Swami and got the satisfaction of a little bit of the sacred throat. The great ones say that wisdom, dispassion, and spiritual qualities have sought their proper place and have chosen Thirukkotiyur Swami as the place to reside. When all other great things are mentioned and the spiritual qualities are discussed, Thirukkotiyur Swami and Navaneetham Swami, the Acharya and the priest of the devotee, are included in the Vedic group.

реиреж. The special feature of Sri Tattva Muktagalapa

Villivalam Swami had the idea of which scripture to offer to Thirukkotiyur Swami. Sri Desikan himself had given the order. In spiritual matters, Sri Desikan created a unique Sri Sukti called Tattva Mukthagalapam, which even the wise men who have obtained the connection of an Acharya and have chosen to attain unshakable clarity in the principles. Some aspects of that book must be mentioned. This Sri Sukti consists of five hundred verses in which he has bestowed his own poetic talent in the Srakthara Vrutta. At the beginning, the Lord makes the prayer for the black color of the Lord Thirumeni into an auspicious verse and at the end, he composes and sings a beautiful final verse in the northern language. Sri Desikan himself has explained the glories of this book and has ordered that it should be learned and internalized. Moreover, he proudly declares that many rare things found in this book, which appears to be the essence of all scriptures, cannot be found in any other book, and that what is not found in this book cannot be found in any other book. He says with great pride and pride that no one except himself, who has grown a hundredfold in knowledge by worshipping the feet of the Lord, can determine the knot tied by Bhagavatra Manujacharya. Therefore, Sri Desikan himself has decided that the disciples should decide the remaining aspects in the manner he has determined and published and that no other principle should be adopted. Think about whether this has been revealed in any other book with this sattvic fervor. реирез. With the Sarvartha Siddhi, Kalakshepa

and then

Tattvamukthagalapam has been revealed and completed. A thought occurred to Sri Desikan. The Lord felt that only by composing a commentary on this difficult text could the devotees gain the true benefit. He also bestowed upon them a commentary called Sarvartha Siddhi, which can easily explain all the meanings. Having attained complete knowledge, Villivalam Swami, with great diligence, received the knowledge of Tattvamukthagalabam with Sarvartha Siddhi from Thirukkotiyur Sri Swami, which enhanced his previous knowledge. Not many even among the best scholars get the opportunity to enjoy these two texts. Since Villivalam Swami had learned these two Suktis thoroughly, the officials in the Swami’s Pravasana would have realized and been delighted with the success he had achieved in the Pilbhu Pravasana. After sitting at the head of that college for many years and performing jnanapradhana, Thirukkottiyur Swami had to retire. Sri Nrusimhan only appoints great men who are not too different from each other as the head of that college.

реиреи. Study of Brahmanism

Villivalam Swami studied Nyaya Shastra thoroughly and with its help earned the qualification that there were no more Suktis to be absorbed in Adhyatma Shastra, but even after he had earned the desire to learn Brahmanism, which is the last part of Nyaya Shastra,

Do you know who was appointed to that position by Srimad Alagya Singha after the retirement of Sri Swami of Thirukkottiyur? That Swami was the Devanar Vilagam Sri-Upalakshmi Narasimhacharya Swami, who was honored as the successor. After serving in the service of Bhagavatara, Aditi Sadkara, Bhagavata Kaingaryam, and as the utsavadi of the Archai Thirumeni in many divine lands, this great man was known for his immense wealth and for his impeccable conduct in the pursuits of knowledge, devotion, and devotion. This holy man, born in the great lineage of those who have been worshipping the shining eye with the sixteen-fold golden Thirumeni, has also experienced and worshipped that eye permanently. He began studying Nyaya Shastra from his father, Navaneetham Sri Swami, and then studied Sathu Shastra Kalpatharu Ammasatram from Sri Swami, and then became a monk.

He achieved great success in the Nyaya Shiromani within four years of joining the college. In the study of Nyaya Shastra, I was fortunate enough to be called Satirthyan by this great man. The Swami’s wealth and broad-mindedness made him accept and run the Sri Madurantakam College as an invaluable resource. It is not necessary to explain here that this great man later adorned the рекрелth Sri Ahobila Asthanam. Our Villivalam Swami, who knew the limits of wisdom, started Brahminism from the new Pradhanathyakshar Swami and studied other scriptures well under his Guru. The leader Swami, who had tasted the Pravasanath, is enthusiastic that he has received such an authority. He bestowed upon him all the excellent books and made it seem as if there was no more book to be learned in the Nyaya Shastra. The special gift that Villivalam Swami was blessed with, so that he could see many things that he had not taught, made him an excellent Naiyayi. He also rejoiced in the merits. Villivalam Swami acquired excellent Nirvaha power in logic and Vedanta and shone as a person worthy of great respect from the Vidvat Koshti.

реирей. Receiving Awards

Seeing Villivalam Swami’s knowledge, power of subject analysis and skill in conducting discourse, many Sadassu gladly invited this Swami and made him participate. Srimad Alagyasingar and Pandit

Brief History

резрей

The group of Thiruvullam had a great opportunity to meet Thiruvullam in the annual Sadassa held at Srimalola Vidvat Sadassa held by Srimad Alagyasingar in Hyderabad many years ago. Thiruvullam was very pleased with the oratory skills of this Swami and bestowed the title of ‘Vedanta Vavathookar’ on him in the midst of the assembly, making the scholars shake their heads. In order to avoid a double reign, Srimad Alagyasingar gave this prestigious award in his own name, making the Swami’s name forgotten. When the eightieth Thiru Nakshatra Purtiya Mahotsavam of Sri Abhinava Ranganatha Brahmadanthra Parakala Swami, who had risen as the incumbent of the Sri Parakala Math in Mysore, composed the Bahu Grantha and became a great scholar, was celebrated with great pomp, our Villivalam Swami was called with great grace and was very happy to see his special knowledge and skill in argumentation. He was bestowed with the title of ‘Vidvanmani’ and was highly praised by that great Acharya.

реирек. Atmaguna Purtiya

Bharat says that the result of acquiring good knowledge is to be filled with good qualities and virtues. The Brahmanas say that all the scriptures prescribe the attainment of restraint as the fruit and that one who has restrained the mind is considered to be knowledgeable of all the scriptures. Just as many good qualities shine forth in Villivalam Swami, restraint has also naturally settled in the heart, which is the gift of Charanya. It is very fitting for this Swami, who, having practiced the eternal duties up to and including aupasana, Bhagavataratanam, Vaishva Devam, etc., and the non-non Even the best scholars in the world, because even the smallest blemishes arising in the heart due to some doubts in the matter of Sampradaya, did not approach Villivalam Swami, therefore, without any room for any feeling of difference, Swami was proud to be known as Sarvabh┼лta Suhrutha with the feeling of being our Ramanuja-Desika-Darshanasthas, which is unique to him. This Swami’s way is also exceptional. Swami’s non-attachment allows even the receiving of the food that the Shastras allow - that which comes to him by itself -

реирен.

Varanasi Residence

Having heard of the special knowledge and power of the Villivalam Swami in various ways, the Kasima City University invited him with desire and love to receive the Swami’s blessings. There was a fear that the Swami would suffer from a lack of morality in going to such a distant land and living. Then the Apthas assured him that he would be able to lead a life without any such deficiency, and the Swami gained some strength. The Swami’s Varanasi residence, which began on the banks of the Ganges, where he was purified by Shankara, who had joined the Satuppuyan Tal from the hand of Satumugan, and had realized that supreme nature, had descended into the Sadaiyin. The Swami was very happy that he had the opportunity to use the Ganga Theertha that he had taken on the first day only for the Ganga Theertha, which our countrymen had discovered and revealed, from bathing to Bhagavatharadhanam.

реирео. Respect for the people of the North towards the Swami

The Swami’s Shastra Pravasanam began in a new way at the university. The scholars of the North, who were well aware of the excellence of knowledge in the South, were very surprised by the style of the Shastra Pravasanam and the power of Villivalam Swami and made them engage with the Swami. Even the feeling of alienation that naturally arises in them from these countries due to the difference of nationality did not arise in the case of the Swami,

It is a rare opportunity that they treated the Swami with great respect and became one with him.

Villivalam Sri Swami’s

Many Sri Vaishnavas who had gone there on pilgrimage from this country were amazed by the rituals performed there and were well received by the Swami and explained those ceremonies. Villivalam Swami, who was always engaged in the sacred service of Vidya Pravasa without any rest or rest, did not care about his physical health and even brought pain to his Lord.

реиреп. Involvement of ancestors in Archai

Considering the experience of the Azhwar Acharyas in Archai Thirumeni, it is natural for Villivalam Swami to be involved in Archai Thirumeni. Nammalvar speaks of his mind, speech, body, and nose as if they were used for the service of the Archai Thirumeni. Then, going a step further and experiencing him here and being united with his qualities, he asks himself whether the Vaikuntam that he gives so much would be enough. The excessive involvement he had in the Archai Thirumeni had led him to the point of denying the eternal existence and even to the point of atheism. Thirupanazhwar’s position is different. He spoke with conviction that even if he saw all the Archai Thirumenis in the Thiruvarangan Thirumeni and brought before his eyes the Param Viyuham-Vibhavam and other Thirumenis, his eyes would not be able to see them when they saw the arena, and our Desikan also explained that Azhwar had a beautiful analogy in mind. That is, a child who grows up on breast milk alone, without artificial feeding, like today. Ku speaks of the state of Thirupanazhvar as if other food is not tasty. He says that even if Thondaradi powders are offered to Thiruvarangan, he does not want it except for the Indra position. Sri Desikan also swears that if the great lord gets the Thirumeniyanubhavam permanently, he will not want Sri Vaikundavasam at all, but he grants it.

рейреж. Villivalam Swami’s involvement in the Archai

Such involvements and his natural experience have resulted in Villivalam Swami not being able to perform the Archai Thirumeniyanubhavam. The inspiration for Archai entered his heart while he was still a student at Tirupati College. As soon as the rest period in the college began, he would come straight to the temple and immerse himself in the experience of what was inside him.

Summary of the story

резрен

It became a habit for Villivalam Swami to stand there, savoring each of his divine limbs, losing his soul in the complete beauty of the Lord, forgetting himself. It can be said that experiencing the Lord deeply during the Archa is an art. Only a few fortunate people can master this art. The state of being immersed in the Archa is a blessing given to this Swami by the Lord. At times, the Almighty would enter the heart of this Swami and invite him to give his experience directly. Immediately, the Swami’s mind would quickly calm down and his body would go to the Perumal temple. It was a commotion to experience the Almighty. He will immerse himself in the experience. He will stand spellbound by the divine beauty of the Thiruvathara branches, which exude the fragrance of the Vapai that Brahma offered with devotion in the Asvamedha Yagama. A vision will arise in the Swami’s heart as if some cool words of grace were being spoken to him from that Thiruvatavazhavai. He will show before his eyes a grandeur that cannot be seen in any other form of worship, and he will captivate the Swami. Villivalam Swami has equal involvement in both the mysteries. He will share in the experience of the divine qualities that the Azhwar experiences by listening to the continuous flow of that bliss with the great one who seeks it from behind. Later, in the Vadamarai group that was searching for the great sage, they fell on their knees and were overjoyed at his greatness. The Swami had a burning desire to visit many divine lands and experience the sacred deities. The Divya Desayatra began. In his youth, Swami visited many places such as Thiruvallikeni Thirukudanthai Thiruvinnakar - Raja Mannar Sannithi and experienced the Lords of each place to the fullest, especially the great Perumal of Thiruvaranga, and immersed himself in the ocean of bliss. рейрез. Sri Ahobila Matham-Acharya Paramparai Speciality

When Sri Desikan expressed his happiness about the Acharya Paramparai he had received and the Acharya relationship, he expressed his great joy at the fact that he was not given a birth as an animal etc., which was bound by karma and could not find a good path, but was given a human birth suitable for him to study the Shastras and do good deeds, and that he was not born in the atheist class, and that he was not born in the class that sees everything as a lie, only the true state of Brahman by using the Vedic name, and that he was not born in the class that sees everything as a lie, and that he was given a birth according to the Sampradaya lineage coming from Villivalam Sri Swami through Madipaliyachan and was taken to the feet of his grandson Apputhurai and guided him to Ujji Vika. He has thanked the Lord and spoken. Having adopted that method, Villivalam Swami also speaks with joy that Sri Lakshminrusimhan has made him a member of the best Sampradayam. In the Sri Sannidhi Parampara, which has had forty-four Yatheeshwaras as Acharyas till date, although Srimad Adhivan Sadagopa Yathindra Mahadesikan was the first Acharya, the first Acharya to give him an Ashram was Ajaliyashinghan. In the previous era, the first person to give him the name Ajaliyashinghan was Thirumazhisai Prana. He concluded by saying, ‘Narasinghan is beautiful, he is the Supreme Personality of Godhead’ and was amazed to see the Lord and advised the world to surrender to his feet. Nammazhvara, however, said that the glory of Narasimhan, who had shown to all things that he was the innermost being, was beyond his imagination. Having thus acquired unique glory, Thirunarasimhan conceived the idea of establishing the Sri Ahobilamadam Sampradayam as a way to worship him as the Yatheeswaras and perform the Acharyagam. He found a great man to appoint as the first Acharya. He selected a perfect brahmacharya who was a perfect authority without any defect. He saw great merit in admitting him, who was still in brahmacharya, to a Sannyasa Ashram that was largely similar to that Ashram. He wanted to give Sannyasa to that great man with his own hands. To qualify for that, he himself took the form of a yati, preached the Presha mantra with his own mouth, and with his own hands bestowed the sacred symbols of Kashyaya and Tridandam, making the great man the first occupant of the throne, and himself also worshipped the Archa-murti, Nammazhvara. The name of Srimad Adhivan Sadagopa Yathindra Mahadesikan was also blessed by the Lord Thirunarasingha, the one who is the embodiment of beauty. From that day until today, that great Sampradayam has been growing and shining ever more because of the Yatheeswarar. Sri Lakshmindra Simha, the Lord of the divine land of Sinhavel Kundra, who has participated in the act of grace, sits in the Astha Nath as an Aaradhya Devi and is growing with the food lovingly fed by the Srimad Alagyasingha. It is only right that Villivalam Swami should be happy and proud that Thirunarasingha has made him a member of such a great Sampradayam!

рейрем. Swami’s Shashtyapta Purthi

Our Villivalam Swami is completing sixty years. Shashtyapta Purthi is considered a great auspicious event in his life.

Summary of History

реирей

We see in the world that even the common people gather their relatives and celebrate this with great pomp, considering it as an auspicious second marriage. The great sages Paramaikandi do not consider this as a sacred duty and do not conduct it as a grand festival without any pomp. But we see that their enlightened disciples, respected friends and loving relatives gather and insist on them, and they get permission to conduct the festival as their duty and conduct it well. That is the situation that developed for our Villivalam Swami. Swami has no intention of doing anything superstitious. Villivalam Swami did not like the fact that, like the flowers that are released today, he gave priority to earning money through advertisements and carried some knowledge and got caught up in the knowledge that some of them praise him. The Swami’s opinion was that along with the daily Bhagavataradhanam, which is performed as a non-jnagaingaryam as permitted by the scriptures, the argyadis could perform the non-jnagaingaryam, which is a form of devotion, in private in his own temple for the Janma Nakshatra, and perform the Shashtyapta Purti in a nominal manner. But the Swami’s apthas, respected good people, and disciples who had entered the pravasanat wanted to conduct this festival with great pomp and began to earn money for it. Knowing this, the Swami did not agree at all and forced them to stop these activities immediately. The asthikas who were trying to stand there were unable to break the Swami’s sanctity. But the sanctity of Sri Nrusimha was different. He thought of celebrating this festival in solitude with his beloved and announced this news through her mouth. If the Swami had known in advance, would he have prevented this too? On seeing this auspicious news published in Sri Nrusimha Priya, even those who were bound by the Swami’s unpretentious and peaceful nature were filled with enthusiasm. Many devotees, with great joy, collected a large amount of money for the completion of the sixth auspicious month without the Swami’s knowledge. This had reached the ears of the Swami. If there were one or two, the Swami would have dared to refuse. They dared to present it to the Swami as ’the money bestowed by the Lord for the Bhagavatharathana’. The Swami was in a difficult situation. They insist that the Vedic recitation, Srimad Ramayanathi Patanam and Bhagavatharathanam should be conducted for five days with the help of selected Vedas. Can these good deeds be denied? The Swami could not refuse the way they performed and had to agree.

рейрен. Shashtyapta Purthi Vaibhavam in Mukkur

S

If this mahotsavam is conducted in the presence of Srimad Aglaya Singhar Thirumu with that divine kataksha and with that supreme grace, then the Swami may have agreed as a swaroopa nuguna. At that time, Srimad Aglaya Singhar Sri Malola along with the residents of Ahobila had arisen there as a result of the fortunate speciality of the people of Ahobila. At that time, Villivalam Swami could not go to Ahobila. Finally, Sri Lakshmi Nrusimha, using her strategy, decided to hold the Swami’s Shashtyapta Purthi Mahotsavam in Mukkur Sri village, which is considered a holy place as the place where Srimad Aglaya Singhar lives. Need I say more? The Mahotsavam begins and continues for five days. Everywhere you look, there is a group of Bhagavatas, who are scholars of the Vedas. The sounds of the Vedas continue to fall sweetly on the ears without interruption. On one side, Srimad Ramayana is being recited. Bhagavatarathanam like Bharadwaja Adityam is being performed. Even then, Swami feels only happiness that these events are happening for him and good deeds are being performed. From Aho Pilath, the divine rays of the Sinhavel Kundudaiyan and the divine grace of the beautiful singer continue to fall. The feeling of being blessed by the presence of the beautiful singer in person arises in the hearts of Villivalam Swami and others and makes them happy. With this, the Shashtyapta Purthi Mahotsavam of Villivalam Swami was celebrated in the month of Aadi in the inauspicious year on the full moon day of Thirunakshatra (рен-рео-ренрем) at Mukkur Srigram. The good people who had come, having fulfilled their desires, happily sang auspicious songs and returned to their village. A certain fortune also befell the young man. Having reached the humble understanding of the greatness of the Swami, the devotee composed and printed six verses in the Srakthara Vrutta and six verses of greetings in Tamil in the Arusirasiri Vrutta with the same idea, and presented them to the Swami, thus receiving the satisfaction of a small act of service. I have become a monk.

рейрео. Composition of treatises

There are many types of treatises composed by scholars. Some treatises seem to convey the philosophy of the Siddhanta. Some treatises condemn the faults of others in our Siddhanta and make us realize the truth. Our Villivalam Swami has composed treatises in both types using his keen intellect. Although some of the principles of Sri Desikan Madhva religion were in conflict with our philosophy, the main

summary of history

реирел

principles of “Srimannarayana is the goddess”, he published that religion as a mother close to our religion due to its non-difference in principle. In response to the book Madhva Chandrika that appeared in that religion, Villivalam Swami has created a book called ‘Madva Chandrika Mohaboham’ and explained the true situation. He wrote a book called ‘Tattva Marthanda Vimarchanam’, which is a counterpoint to the book ‘Tattva Marthanda Kriya Vidhunanam’ and rejected its research. He translated the Srimad Ramayana single verse into the vernacular and explained it so that the people of the north could also understand and enjoy its essence. Having found a foothold in Advaita philosophy, he published books like Advaita Siddhi The Lord gave the Swami the opportunity to compose a commentary on the great book ‘Advaita Ratnarakshanam’ by Madhusudhana Saraswati, who was a great scholar in our community, who composed many books on Shastra and Siddhanta, who has done many special services to Sanskrit and our Siddhanta, and who shines as a Kirti Seshara. Seeing that Pandita Raja Thiruvarangam Sri Upa. Tirumalai Dadacharya Swami (D. T. Swami) Villivalam Swami was the right authority, He called him and with His utmost grace appointed him to write a commentary on that book by Madhusudhana Saraswati. Villivalam Swami happily accepted the Swami’s order and composed a great treatise called ‘Advaita Ratna Tattva Pariksha’. Only after all these treatises were printed by Bhagavat Sankalpa, can the rasika scholars realize their greatness and experience their essence. When Swami was in Kashi, he wrote many Vyasams on the titles ‘Upadaantatriveni’, ‘Pratipimba Tattva Krilam’, ‘Nadva Prayojagadva Visaram’ etc. published in the monthly magazines published by Kashi Vishva Vidyalaya at his request. Those who were there experienced and highly appreciated it.

рейреп. Origin of Manipravala Style

Sri Desikan explained the three principles - three secrets - that the laymen should know in order to benefit not only those who are versed in the Shastras but also the common officers, through many secrets in Manipravala style. Manipravala is a beautiful work in the blend of Northern and Tamil. It was first composed by Thirukurugai Prana Pillan, an Acharya who was a direct disciple of Emperum─Бn─Бr. By the appointment of Sri Bhashyakar, he had the commentary on Thiruvaimozhi in the Manipravala style called Thiruvarairapadi in the presence of Sri Bhashyakar, and when he was very pleased with Thiruvullam, then by his appointment,

F-рен

реирем

Villivalam Sri Swami’s

Pillan gave this Sukti to the world. It is not known that any book appeared in the Manipravala style before this. It cannot be denied that this was the guide for the various commentary that was to appear later. After him, many Acharyas followed this method and created many Suttis in the Manipravala style itself. This style is very influential in the Sampradayam. Sri Vaishnavas of all castes

are the means by which they experience and enjoy the blessings of time through the Rahasyas and other Manipravala Suktis. When Sri Desikan was revealing the Rahasyas for the benefit of everyone, the book of Rahasyas called Paramatapangam also appeared from Swami Thiruvakki. This is a very comprehensive Rahasya. рекреж. Structure of Paramatapangam Rahasya

Let us discuss the structure of this Rahasya. First, an auspicious verse to the divine hero Thiruvaindhai. Then Sri Desikan prays to Thiruvaliyazhvan, who is seen with eight hands, to grant him the power to condemn other religions. It is the tradition of the ancestors to first pray to Thiruvaliyazhvan to achieve success in any endeavor. Then Sri Desikan recounts the benefits rendered by the Acharyas. Then, embracing our philosophy, he explains the three principles of Cetanam - Asetanam - Ishvara. He explains the need to condemn the principles of other religions and shows the common faults in them. Then, by stating and condemning the main principles of the Charvaga religion - the four types of Buddhism - Advaita religion - Jainism - Bhaskara Yadava religion - Vaiyakarana religion - Ganadham religion - Pasupada religion, he speaks of the greatness of the Pancharatra Shastra, explains the nature of surrender, and states that the Sampradaya that comes through our Acharyas is the best. Finally, our Desikan completes this Rahasya Granth by praising the sixteen Tirukhas of Thiruvaliyazhva, who completely defeated the Kandanata of other religions. In accordance with the order of Rahasya Granths, in this Rahasya, he has revealed the pasurams containing the concept of each chapter at the beginning and end. Those pasurams alone are called Paramata Bangam. It has been given as a Prabandham in the Sri Desika Prabandham and is also being continued.

рекрез. Paramatapangam is a difficult Sri Sukti

Although this mystery was revealed in the style of Manipravala, its difficulty is immeasurable. Only those who are proficient in general sciences such as logic and have gone deep into Vedanta can enjoy this mystery and enjoy knowing things. If Swami Desika had revealed this book in the Sanskrit language itself, it would have joined the class of books like Sarvartha Siddhi Nyaya Sitthanjanam Satadushani and would have acquired the name of being more difficult than them and would have been useful only to special scholars. Unlike those scriptures, those who really want to know the reason why this scripture was revealed in the Manipravala style can only go to Nithya Vibhuti one day after a long time and ask Sri Desika himself, who is the leader of the Nithya Surigas - the liberated ones - and is in the perfect Bhagavadana experience. When ordinary officials, thinking of it as having the name Manipravarlam, take the Paramatha Panga in their hands, what they understand is the Tamil viguti at the end of each verse. Due to its difficult nature, it has remained somewhat hidden from the public and not caught up in the pravasana and publicity like other mysteries. Some laymen have even started giving it the names Paramapada Panga - Paramapanga - Paramartha Panga. Many great predecessors did not get the opportunity to compose a commentary on it.

рекреи. The creation of a commentary on the Paramatapanga

Now Sri Lakshmi Nrusimhan thought of a comprehensive commentary on this. The enthusiasm and guidance of Sri Upa. D.T. Dadacharya Swami encouraged our Villivalam Swami. The help of the Nyaya Sastra, which Sri Upa. Uttamur Abhinavadesika Swami had completely acquired, was the reason for creating a new commentary. Only good commentators know how much difficulty there is in composing a commentary so that everyone can clearly understand the meaning of the original text. There is not much difficulty in composing original texts independently. Taking this difficulty into account, Sri Desika did not hesitate to entrust the responsibility of commenting on some of the difficult texts he had revealed to others, but he himself wrote the commentary. Our Villivalam Swami has embarked on the difficult task of creating a commentary on the Paramatham Bandha called Manipravalam. There is a special reason why this work, which this Swami started with the instructions of the elders and the prayers of the Suhruts, the aptars, was completed in a good manner. Acharya Sarva Bhoumarai, who firmly convinced the world that any good work that begins with his Sankalpa or with his Anugraha Viresham, which has adopted the Sankalpa of Sri Nrusimhan, is not at all

many

реирео

Villivalam Sri Swami, is not

the

Olam of Sri Rat Alagya Singha, who now adorns the Astha Nagata, is the primary reason for the success of this work. The Sri Sannidhi Srimukha, who appeared with perfect gadhakshad and the greatness of the Lord, is the proof of this.

рекрей. Special features in the text

The text itself is full of so many special features! The fact that the respective religions have searched for and cited the scriptures when addressing the Prakaranas criticizing other religions is a great feature. The fact that the avatars appropriate to each word of the original are given is very beneficial for the understanding of the meaning. The text also does not fail to give the appropriate parayoi to the words used by Sri Desigal. The fact that the Swami’s opinion is explained for each word of the original is also captivating. In some places, the fact that he has raised objections and disputed and effectively stated the appropriate lamathan is a great feat. What more feature does a text need? The name of this commentary is also very appropriate. The answer to the question of whether Sri Desikan’s ideas came naturally to this text because Vilavivalam Swami gave it that name, or whether he gave it the name because he saw Sri Desikan’s ideas reflected in it, is that both options are possible.

рекрек. Villivalam Swami’s Preface

Bhagirathan worked hard and brought the Ganges and gave it to us. Vilvivalam Swami, who lived on the banks of the Ganges for many years and refined his knowledge and wisdom through the use of the Sastharapravasata, brought the Paramatapanga Vyakyada Granth from a single section like a flood of the Ganges and made us experience and bathe in it. After giving his intellect and body an immense amount of work and engaging in a great activity, Thirumeni’s health deteriorated. Despite the hardships, he completed it with enthusiasm. With the special support of the present Shriyat Alagyasingar, who was in accordance with his authority, and with the financial assistance of many devotees, it was possible to publish the first part of the commentary, which consists of ten chapters. In it, Villivalam Swami himself wrote a detailed preface. He has written. From the explanation given in it for many things,

Abstract of History

реиреж

Swami’s soul-nature-knowledge-mainly modesty-humility-and all the efforts in this great work can be clearly understood. Also, due to some printing errors due to his physical condition-defects in the notes etc., he was saddened and asked for forgiveness through his own mouth. Although Villivalam Swami was not completely satisfied with the composition of the first part, he was happy that it was well composed without any defects in the details.

рекрел. Swami’s Division-Responsibility of the Younger

The text of ten chapters has been completed in the first part. Explanations for the remaining fourteen chapters should be published as the second part. Swami Magnani was keen to publish this part with great care and complete scrutiny. But the Sarayan Thiruvullam had taken root. Satisfied with the fact that an explanation of the Paramatham Banga had emerged in a manner that had never been published before and that the first part had been published, Paramapathanathan wanted to give his complete experience in Nithya Vibhuti and took Swami Vilalivalam with him. If Swami had lived in this Leela Vibhuti for some more time, what further benefits would have accrued to Siddhantha and Sampra Taayat, and what loss our culture has suffered due to Swami’s unexpected departure, our hearts warm. The Lord has found and shown us a way to somewhat reduce the sorrow of Swami’s departure and to publish the second part of the Paramatham Banga. In the Jnana-Anushta Nadis and in the creation of Vyasa and in the creation of Upanyasa, the young Villivalam Krishnamacharya Swami, who mostly adopted Vilviyala Swami, has brought out the second part of Paramatapanga in a clean and beautiful manner, considering it our duty to complete the work done by our Thiruntamayanar. It is a great blessing for the world to test and publish it in a proper manner without any room for the minor errors that were encountered in the first part. рекрем. Publication of the Second Part of Paramatapanga

I am very happy to submit that the main reason for the publication of the second part of Paramatapanga with this rare commentary is that the present Srimad Aglaya Singer Divyakataksha has blessed us with a special melody. In this work, the divine grace and necessity of our Srimad Alagyasingar were well understood and some devotees also provided financial support with diligence. In the development of our philosophy,

F-рео

рейреж

Villivalam Sri Swami’s

efforts have been used to create this book, which can easily show Sri Desikasayam to the scholars who enjoy it. It is very appropriate that Sri Lakshminrusimhan Sankalpa and Injimedu Srimad Alagyasingar, the present Srimad Alagyasingar, jointly created this book with the divine grace of two great Acharyas, Sri Lakshminrusimhan Sankalpa and Srimad Alagyasingar of Injimedu. This book, which Villivalam Swami has painstakingly produced and specially used his intellectual power, is a great gift to the Sri Vaishnava community and its descendants. It is an important duty for every Sri Vaishnava to purchase this two-part Sri Kosam and adorn his home with this divine Sukti of Sri Desika, without thinking about his own worthiness or unworthiness to read and understand this book. There is no doubt that Villivalam Swami, who, regardless of his physical weakness, held his life in one hand and sacrificed himself by offering this book with the other hand, will complete this complete Sri Kosam with the great effort of his son Thiruth Thambiyar, including the second part to be published, in the eternal vibhuti before Sri Desikan Thirumu, to Sri Lakshmindu Simha, the Supreme Lord, and will receive the praise of the divine couple and the eternally liberated.

рекрен. A great blessing

Here is a very important aspect. Now, on the auspicious day of the incarnation of Srimad Alagya Singhar, who is now the Acharya Sarva Bhumara in the Astana, and on the auspicious day of the completion of Srimalola Vidvat Sadassa, Sri Ramanujadaya Bhadra, who is eternally blessed for us, and on the auspicious day of the incarnation of Avani Hastha Menum, the great meritorious day, Sri Upa, Krishnamacharya Swami, with utmost devotion, offers the second part of Sri Paramatapanga Vyakiyanam, a special work of his brother, in the presence of Srimad Alagya Singhar, and with the utmost grace, what greater blessing could there be than to have the second part of Sri Paramatapanga Vyakiyanam, a special work of his brother, appear before the world with those hands in the presence of great scholars?

рекрео. The Complete Speech of the Adiyen

By his many virtues, reminding his Reverend Father in many ways, and emphasizing that he is the greatest Suhrut for the Adiyena for many years, Sri Ahobilamadam Asthana Vidwan Sri Upa. Villivalam Krishnamacharya Swami, who primarily seeks the welfare of the Adiyena, through the services he is doing, makes him forget the separation of the Reverend Father somewhat. Summary of the History

рейрез

Krin. Paramat Panka Vyakiyana Nirmaana Ilaval Swami kindly ordered me to draw a Vyasam about the great work done by Villivalam Swami through the gate. I have drawn this as a work of art suitable to my form, and I have reached the level of my understanding, and I have enjoyed the inner nature of a water-drenched squirrel who has bathed and run around. Having attained the spiritual satisfaction that has been achieved by the order of my dear Ilaval Swami, I have become a Kruda-jna, a Kruda-kruda, a Kruda-dhartha.
